data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.0">FC Dallas 2, Portland Timbers 2 | MLS Cup Playoffs Match Recap</h1><div class="byline" data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1"><address class="author" data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.0"><a data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.0.0" href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/author/Scott Sidway" rel="author">Scott Sidway</a></address><time class="pubdate" data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.1" datetime="2015-11-29">Nov 29, 2015</time></div><div data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.2"></div><div data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.3" id="ooyala-player-drM2w3eTqXzl4V1cP-7u8YTHjYAKr7n-"></div><div class="gigya-share" data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.4" id="article-share"></div><img class="article-primary-image" data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.5" src="http://league-mp7static.mlsdigital.net/styles/image_default/s3/images/Adi-celebration.jpg"><article class="article" data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.6"><p>FRISCO, Texas -\xc2\xa0After a scorching run through the end of the season and the Audi MLS Cup Playoffs, the Portland Timbers have booked their first-ever berth in the MLS Cup.</p>\n<p>While needing at least two goals to advance or force extra time, Dallas played the roles of the aggressors in the first half, but still missed on a handful of chances in the final third. The two teams would go into half deadlocked at 0-0.</p>\n<p>After the break, <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/fanendo-adi">Fanendo\xc2\xa0Adi</a> found himself in prime position in the 54th\xc2\xa0minute to all but seal Portland\xe2\x80\x99s trip to either Columbus or New York next weekend. After working the right flank, <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/diego-valeri">Diego Valeri</a> found Adi alone in front of the net with Dallas defender <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/walker-zimmerman">Walker Zimmerman</a> on the ground. Adi was able to fire the ball off of <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/jesse-gonzalez">Jesse Gonzalez</a>\xe2\x80\x99s right foot, ricocheting into the net for 1-0 lead. Zimmerman was making only his third start since mid-June in place of <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/zach-loyd">Zach Loyd</a>.</p>\n<ul>\n<li><a href="http://matchcenter.mlssoccer.com/matchcenter/2015-11-29-fc-dallas-vs-portland-timbers/boxscore"><strong>FULL BOXSCORE AND CHALKBOARD</strong></a></li>\n</ul>\n<p>Dallas would not give up, however. After being on the defensive often in the first half, defender <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/ryan-hollingshead">Ryan Hollingshead</a> found the back of the net in the 69th\xc2\xa0minute. Argentine midfielder <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/mauro-diaz">Mauro Diaz</a> took a pass from <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/jevaughn-watson">Je-Vaughn Watson</a> at the top of the Portland box and found Hollingshead streaking down the left flank. Hollingshead drilled the ball to the opposite corner, squeaking it inside the left post to draw even at 1-1.</p>\n<p>Just four minutes later in the 72nd\xc2\xa0minute, Diaz was able to thread another high-arcing pass, this time off a free kick. The ball found the head of a charging <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/blas-perez">Blas Perez</a>, who substituted into the game in the 66th\xc2\xa0minute, and he put it past <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/adam-kwarasey">Adam Kwarasey</a> to give Dallas a 2-1 lead and a hope of forcing extra time.</p>\n<ul>\n<li><a href="http://matchcenter.mlssoccer.com/matchcenter/2015-11-29-fc-dallas-vs-portland-timbers/stats"><strong>CHECK OUT STATS FROM DAL-POR</strong></a></li>\n</ul>\n<p>But the two quick goals in a four minute span was all Dallas was able to muster, as Portland hung tough through the final 20 minutes. Dallas threw out all the stops, including subbing in <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/michel-garbini-pereira">Michel</a> for Hollingshead in the 86th\xc2\xa0minute to attempt to capitalize on set piece opportunities.</p>\n<p>Forward <a href="http://mlssoccer.com/players/lucas-melano">Lucas Melano</a> was able to add a cushion goal in stoppage time after the furious Dallas rally, leaving\xc2\xa0the score level at 2-2.</p>\n<p>They will await the winner of Columbus Crew SC and the New York Red Bulls for their opponent in the MLS Cup next week (4 pm ET; ESPN/UniM\xc3\xa1s in US; TSN/RDS in Canada).</p>\n</article><div class="gigya-comments" data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.8" id="article-comments"></div></img></div></div><div class="ad-wrapper" data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.1" id="matchcenter-recap-1"></div></div></div></section></div></section></main><div class="connection-warning" data-reactid=".lp5ll2hvk0.a" style="pointer-events:none;">Connection Lost.
